       1075838985,    1075851044,  case dfs.type when 'PS' then t.filestream_data_space_id else NULL end,

FROM sys.indexes i

       1075838985,    1075849418,  i.is_padded,
       1075838985,    1075850538,  i.allow_row_locks,
       1075838985,    1075850537,  i.allow_page_locks,
       1075838985,    1075849414,  i.ignore_dup_key,
       1075838985,    1075850574,  i.is_disabled,
       1075838985,    1075850675,  case ds.type when 'FG' then i.data_space_id else NULL end,
       1075838985,    1075850212,  k.name,
       1075838985,    1075851043,  case dfs.type when 'FD' then case when t.filestream_data_space_id > 0 then t.filestream_data_space_id end else NULL end,
       1075838985,    1075851044,  case dfs.type when 'PS' then t.filestream_data_space_id else NULL end,
       1075838985,    1075849143,  case i.has_filter when 1 then i.filter_definition else NULL end,
       1075838985,    1075849420,  case s.no_recompute when 1 then cast( 1 as bit ) else cast( 0 as bit ) end,
       1075838985,    1075852286,  case i.type when 7 then cast( 1 as bit ) else cast( 0 as bit ) end,
       1075838985,    1075852292,  case i.type when 7 then hi.bucket_count else 1 end,
       1075838985,    1075853379,  CASE WHEN i.optimize_for_sequential_key = 1 THEN 'ON' ELSE 'OFF' END 
FROM sys.indexes i 
LEFT OUTER JOIN sys.partitions p on i.object_id = p.object_id and i.index_id = p.index_id 
LEFT OUTER JOIN sys.key_constraints k on i.object_id = k.parent_object_id and i.index_id = k.unique_index_id 
LEFT OUTER JOIN sys.data_spaces ds on ds.data_space_id = i.data_space_id 
LEFT OUTER JOIN sys.tables t on t.object_id = i.object_id 
LEFT OUTER JOIN sys.data_spaces dfs on dfs.data_space_id = t.filestream_data_space_id 
LEFT OUTER JOIN sys.stats s on s.object_id = i.object_id and i.index_id = s.stats_id 
LEFT OUTER JOIN sys.hash_indexes hi on i.object_id = hi.object_id and i.index_id = hi.index_id 
WHERE i.is_primary_key = 1 AND i.type <> 5 AND i.type <> 6 AND i.object_id = 1269579561

FROM sys.indexes i

       1075838985,    1075849413,  case when i.fill_factor = 0 then NULL else i.fill_factor end,
       1075838985,    1075849418,  i.is_padded,
       1075838985,    1075850538,  i.allow_row_locks,
       1075838985,    1075850537,  i.allow_page_locks,
       1075838985,    1075849414,  i.ignore_dup_key,

       1075838985,    1075850675,  case ds.type when 'FG' then i.data_space_id else NULL end,
       1075838985,    1075853379,  CASE WHEN i.optimize_for_sequential_key = 1 THEN 'ON' ELSE 'OFF' END 
FROM sys.indexes i 
LEFT OUTER JOIN sys.key_constraints k on i.object_id = k.parent_object_id and i.index_id = k.unique_index_id

FROM sys.indexes i 
LEFT OUTER JOIN sys.key_constraints k on i.object_id = k.parent_object_id and i.index_id = k.unique_index_id 
LEFT OUTER JOIN sys.data_spaces ds on ds.data_space_id = i.data_space_id 
WHERE i.is_primary_key = 0 AND i.name is not null AND i.type <> 3 AND i.object_id = 1157579162 
ORDER BY i.index_id

       1075839021,    1075850656,  am.assembly_id,
       1075839021,    1075850692,  am.assembly_method,
       1075839021,    1075850563,  am.assembly_class,

       1075839021,    1075850674,  case when tr.type = 'TR' and sm.execute_as_principal_id is NULL then 'CALLER' when tr.type = 'TA' and am.execute_as_principal_id is NULL then 'CALLER' when tr.type = 'TR' and sm.execute_as_principal_id = '-2'  then 'OWNER' when tr.type = 'TA' and am.execute_as_principal_id = '-2'  then 'OWNER' else 'USER' end,

SELECT DISTINCT 
       1075838985,    1073742126,  i.name,
       1075838985,    1075849133,  i.index_id,
       1075838985,    1075849004,  case i.is_unique when 1 then 'AK' else 'IE' end,
       1075838985,    1075850519,  case i.type when 1 then cast( 1 as bit ) else cast( 0 as bit ) end,
       1075838985,    1075849413,  case when i.fill_factor = 0 then NULL else i.fill_factor end,
       1075838985,    1075849418,  i.is_padded,
       1075838985,    1075850538,  i.allow_row_locks,
       1075838985,    1075850537,  i.allow_page_locks,
       1075838985,    1075849414,  i.ignore_dup_key,
       1075838985,    1075850574,  i.is_disabled,
       1075838985,    1075850675,  case ds.type when 'FG' then i.data_space_id else NULL end,
       1075838985,    1075853379,  CASE WHEN i.optimize_for_sequential_key = 1 THEN 'ON' ELSE 'OFF' END 
FROM sys.indexes i 
LEFT OUTER JOIN sys.key_constraints k on i.object_id = k.parent_object_id and i.index_id = k.unique_index_id 
LEFT OUTER JOIN sys.data_spaces ds on ds.data_space_id = i.data_space_id 
WHERE i.is_primary_key = 0 AND i.name is not null AND i.type <> 3 AND i.object_id = 1317579732 
ORDER BY i.index_id
--Parameter 1 = 1317579732
--[2022-10-24 16:02:04] Return from Query - 0 rows

       1075839021,    1075849133,  tr.object_id,
       1075839021,    1075848978,  (select type from sys.events where object_id = tr.object_id and type = 1),
       1075839021,    1075848978,  (select type from sys.events where object_id = tr.object_id and type = 2),
       1075839021,    1075848978,  (select type from sys.events where object_id = tr.object_id and type = 3),
       1075839021,    1075849722,  case when tr.is_not_for_replication IS NOT NULL THEN tr.is_not_for_replication ELSE 2 END,
       1075839021,    1075850656,  am.assembly_id,
       1075839021,    1075850692,  am.assembly_method,
       1075839021,    1075850563,  am.assembly_class,
       1075839021,    1075850670,  case when am.object_id is not NULL then NULL when sm.definition is NULL then cast ( 1 as bit ) else cast ( 0 as bit ) end,
       1075839021,    1075850674,  case when tr.type = 'TR' and sm.execute_as_principal_id is NULL then 'CALLER' when tr.type = 'TA' and am.execute_as_principal_id is NULL then 'CALLER' when tr.type = 'TR' and sm.execute_as_principal_id = '-2'  then 'OWNER' when tr.type = 'TA' and am.execute_as_principal_id = '-2'  then 'OWNER' else 'USER' end,
       1075839021,    1075850838,  case when tr.type = 'TR' and sm.execute_as_principal_id <> '-2' then sm.execute_as_principal_id when tr.type = 'TA' and am.execute_as_principal_id <> '-2' then am.execute_as_principal_id else NULL end,
       1075839021,    1075848990,  tr.is_disabled,
       1075839021,    1075850664,  tr.type ,
       1075839021,    1075848996,  sm.definition,
       1075839021,    1075848991,  tr.is_instead_of_trigger 
FROM sys.triggers tr

LEFT OUTER JOIN sys.objects so on tr.object_id = so.object_id 
LEFT OUTER JOIN sys.sql_modules sm on tr.object_id = sm.object_id 
WHERE tr.parent_id = 1317579732
